### Post by Constantinopolitan on 2015-03-20
Dear all,

I'm a computer illiterate, but nevertheless managed to install Kubuntu 14.10 (or 04, not sure) on my laptop. Now I am trying to make my printer hp professional 1102w work, and that's a big challenge. I downloaded hplip-3.15.2 but installation refuses to work.
When trying to execute it on Konsole, I get the message "Could not find /home/constantinopolitana/Escritorio/hplip.run, starting /bin/bash instead. Please check your profile settings.
I looked at my profile settings but don't get what is wrong there.
Then I tried /bin/bash, and I either get the answer:
No such file or directory (but I write exactly the path indicated in the message above) or I get, when trying to open it from the "downloads", the following message:
I write:
/home/constantinopolitana/Descargas/hplip-3.15.2(2).run, 
and the system answers:
bash: syntax error near unexpected token '2'.

I googled a lot and looked in lots of forums, but I didn't get any information I could understand and/ or use.

Thanks a lot in advance for helping me!

Eva

---

### Post by Y^2om&amp;#7sgP on 2015-03-20
Once you have downloaded the file  HPLIP-3.15.2.run  you need to go to the correct folder in Konsole (I use Xubuntu so for me it's terminal)

Simplest way for me is to use my file explorer to get to the folder, and then on right click, open terminal here, not sure about Kubuntu but I assume you can do something very similar.

Once in the Konsole (terminal) you need to execute the command

sh   hplip-3.15.2.run

Be careful to type the filename _exactly_ as it appears in the download folder.

This should start the whole process, and it will ask then for your user password.

I installed my HP printer using this, and it takes a while, but just accept the defaults and it works well

---

Dear Hattpa,

thanks a lot for the quick reply. When I click the file in file explorer, there is under "actions" the option "execute with konsole". That's what I did before and tried again.
For me it's hplip-3.15.2(2); there was some bug in the first two downloads. Now I did that (after writing /bin/bash), writing 
sh hplip-3.15.2(2).run
and I am again confronted with the syntax error, this time "near unexpected token '(' ". 

There is a detailed description under [http://hplipopensource.com/hplip-web/install/install/index.html](http://hplipopensource.com/hplip-web/install/install/index.html), but I simply don't get beyond the first stage.
I managed to install the same driver under Linux Mint for my previous computer, but now I'm lost.

Best regards,

Eva

### Post by Y^2om&amp;#7sgP on 2015-03-20
It looks like you've downloaded a couple of times

The HP filename from their site is hplip-3.15.2.run

Maybe start from scratch, delete any copies of hplip you already have and then download a fresh copy and start over?  Or of course, just rename the file you have, and just remove the (2) ;)

### Post by Y^2om&amp;#7sgP on 2015-03-20
Alternately, here's a link to a how to

[http://ubuntuhandbook.org/index.php/2013/09/install-hp-linux-printer-driver-in-ubuntu/](http://ubuntuhandbook.org/index.php/2013/09/install-hp-linux-printer-driver-in-ubuntu/)

At the point where it refers to hplip-3.13.9 just change to hplip-3.15.2

Then should be good to go

### Post by Constantinopolitan on 2015-03-20
Hi,

just when I wanted to copy & paste again the screenshot from the Konsole, it started to work with the link you provided me.
There was still an initial problem; apparently the system does not understand that "downloads" and "descargas" is one and the same thing...but when I replaced the former with the latter, YES!, it worked!
I installed the printer and did some trial prints, great!
The only, but minimal and negligible, problem is that the printer does not recognise wireless but only works with the USB connection. But I don't mind that.

Thanks a lot for your support!

Eva
